## SLICE 29 SUMMARY

**Shipped:** CLI voice input (STT) — `src/voice/` transcribes a mic capture (`--voice`, tap-to-toggle) or a file (`--voice-in <path>`) and splices the text into the `chat` prompt exactly like `--audio`'s existing text-splice. Engine: **sherpa-onnx** (`sherpa-onnx-node` N-API addon), model: **moonshine-tiny-en** default (`sherpa-onnx-moonshine-tiny-en-int8`, `bun run setup:voice`), `AGENT_VOICE_STT_MODEL`-overridable (e.g. to moonshine-base-en). Transcription runs behind an execution seam: **in-process** (default — the Task-1 spike confirmed the addon loads under Bun) or a **node-subprocess** worker (`stt-worker.mjs`, `AGENT_VOICE_EXEC=subprocess`). Mic auto-stop uses ffmpeg `silencedetect` (speech-then-pause heuristic), not a real-time VAD model. Degrade-never-crash throughout (missing model/addon/capture failure/silence → warning + `DegradeKind.ToolSkipped` ledger entry, never a crash). New env vars: `AGENT_VOICE_DIR`, `AGENT_VOICE_STT_MODEL`, `AGENT_FFMPEG_CMD`, `AGENT_VOICE_EXEC`, `AGENT_MIC_INDEX` (+ reused `AGENT_MEDIA_TIMEOUT_MS`, voice default 30s). New telemetry: `voice.transcribe` span + `VOICE_STT_MODEL`/`VOICE_CAPTURE_SOURCE`/`VOICE_AUDIO_SECONDS`/`VOICE_DURATION_MS`/`VOICE_OUTCOME` attrs. Scope excludes voice-out/barge-in/streaming/true hold-to-talk — Slice 30 (browser UI, real `getUserMedia` AEC + `keydown`/`keyup`).

**Decisions D1–D8 (+ the silencedetect refinement):**
- D1: transcribe execution seam defaults to **in-process** `sherpa-onnx-node` (Task-1 spike confirmed it loads under Bun); `AGENT_VOICE_EXEC=subprocess` is the one-flag escape hatch to a node worker.
- D2: engine choice **sherpa-onnx** over parakeet-mlx/whisper.cpp alternatives, specifically for its browser-WASM build — reused by Slice 30's web UI with zero second STT stack.
- D3: default model **moonshine-tiny-en** (smallest/fastest of the family) via the sherpa-onnx `asr-models` GitHub release, not HuggingFace — no auth/consent gate needed, unlike the media-gen catalog.
- D4: voice runs **before** media ingest in `chat.ts` so a transcript is part of the raw prompt before `--image`/`--audio`/`--video`/path-auto-detect see it.
- D5: `ingestVoice` is **degrade-never-crash** internally (per-source try/catch), but deps *construction* (building the real `Transcriber`, which loads the addon/model) sits in `chat.ts`'s own outer try/catch, since a missing model/addon throws before `ingestVoice`'s internal degrade logic ever runs — both collapse to the same "warn + continue with the non-voice prompt" outcome.
- D6: mic capture is a **tap-to-toggle** state machine (not push-to-talk) — terminals have no reliable key-release event, so hold-to-talk is deferred to the browser (real `keydown`/`keyup`).
- D7: mic capture hard-caps at `MAX_CAPTURE_SECONDS=60` regardless of stop signal, so the buffer JSON-serialized to the subprocess worker can't grow unbounded.
- D8: voice's own timeout default (30s) is **distinct** from media's (10 min) but **reuses the same env knob** (`AGENT_MEDIA_TIMEOUT_MS`) rather than inventing a voice-only variable — an interactive capture/transcribe turn should fail fast, not inherit a generous batch-generation default.
- **Silencedetect refinement (disclosed, not a deviation from what was asked — a documented implementation choice):** the original Slice-29 re-scope discussion mentioned Silero VAD for auto-stop; what shipped is ffmpeg's `silencedetect` audio filter watching the live capture's stderr instead — model-free and independent of the in-process/subprocess transcribe seam, since it runs entirely inside the ffmpeg process already spawned to get PCM off the mic. Best-effort only: manual `[space]`/`[enter]` and the `MAX_CAPTURE_SAMPLES` cap remain the correctness backstops if `silencedetect` never fires.

**Live-verify:** Task 13 (gated, not yet run as of this ledger entry — real mic, real ffmpeg `avfoundation`, real `sherpa-onnx-node` addon).

**Current suite: 1077 pass / 30 skip / 0 fail** (full `bun run check` — docs:check + typecheck + lint + tests — green through Task 11/12).

CAUGHT+FIXED CRITICAL: capture.ts Response.bytes() on Bun 1.3.11 returns non-Uint8Array -> zero-copy -> every capture transcribed "" silently; fixed via .arrayBuffer()+Uint8Array. ## SLICE 30b — PHASE 8 · SECURITY FAST-FOLLOW (telemetry token URL→body)
- [x] Fast-follow (post-land on `main`): a push-time security review flagged (MEDIUM) that the voice telemetry beacon put the session token in the URL (`?k=<token>`) — leaks via browser history + proxy access-logs once the app is served beyond localhost (a standing future requirement). FIX: moved the token OUT of the URL into the `sendBeacon` request BODY, handler self-authenticating. `beacon.ts` now POSTs plain `/api/telemetry` with `{ token, event }` (fire-and-forget try/catch unchanged). `handler.ts` reads the body, verifies the token TIMING-SAFE FIRST via a new `TokenGuard.verifyToken(raw)` (reuses the shared constant-time `matches()`, no `===`) → 401 on missing/wrong (no span, no body echo, token never logged/spanned); only then validates `event` against `TelemetryEventSchema` (400) and writes the span (fire-and-forget catch still → 204). `app.ts` perimeter now lets `POST /api/telemetry` past the shared HEADER guard (the handler owns the token check) — but the **Host/Origin perimeter (`enforcePerimeter`) still fronts it exactly as before**, and every OTHER route still requires the header bearer; the `?k=`/`verifyQuery` special-case is deleted. `token.ts` dropped `verifyQuery` (+ `?k=` reading), added `verifyToken`. Tests updated + proven: server telemetry route (valid body-token→204+span, wrong/missing→401 no span, invalid event→400, span-throw→204), token.test (verifyToken constant-time), app.test (`?k=` honored NOWHERE incl. /api/telemetry, other routes still header-only, Host/Origin still fronts /api/telemetry + cross-origin→403), web beacon.test (URL is `/api/telemetry` NO `?k=`, body carries `{token,event}`). Gates: root typecheck+lint green, `bun test tests/server tests/contracts` (1 unrelated pre-existing live-model builder flake), web typecheck + beacon test green, biome check --write, docs:check green. 4 doc surfaces updated (architecture.md Telemetry §, ROADMAP Phase-8 + gap-row, README 2 spots) — `?k=` wording → body-token, handler-verified timing-safe. Perimeter model preserved cleanly (Host/Origin unchanged; only bearer/token check relocated for the one beacon route).
- [x] SECURITY fast-follow (commit 736be06): voice telemetry token moved URL(?k=)→sendBeacon BODY; handler self-authenticates via constant-time verifyToken BEFORE schema-validation (401 no-span on bad/missing), Host/Origin enforcePerimeter still fronts /api/telemetry (cross-origin→403), bearer header still guards every other route, ?k=/verifyQuery deleted, token never logged/spanned/echoed. Pre-empts the remote-access URL-leak. 25 server/contract tests + web 348 green. Docs (architecture/ROADMAP/README auth wording) updated.
- [x] FABLE CAPSTONE (top-tier final gate, per [[feedback-background-agents-and-fable]]): SECURITY = MERGE-READY (all vectors traced clean); WHOLE-BRANCH CAPSTONE = SHIP (voice hook T9–14+T22+I1 composes, rtf non-zero e2e; telemetry shapes agree; chat.run reach complete + TERMINAL_RUN_ROOTS single-sourced; a11y genuine WCAG-AA not just axe; capability flip 🟡→✅ justified, all 8 phases real).
